function isEmpty(s){
	return ((s == null) || (s.length == 0))
}
function isInBag(s,bag){
  var i;
  for (i = 0; i < s.length; i++){
    var c = s.charAt(i);
    if (bag.indexOf(c) == -1) return false;
  }
  return true;
}
function isNotInBag(s,bag){
  var i;
  for (i = 0; i < s.length; i++){
    var c = s.charAt(i);
    if (bag.indexOf(c) > -1) return false;
  }
  return true;
}
function isGoodChar(str){
  if (isNotInBag(str," -_.><,[]{}?/+=|\\'\":;~!@#$%^&()`")) return true;
  else return false;
}
function isNumber(str){
  if (isInBag(str,"0123456789")) return true;
  else return false;
}
function isLetter(str){
  if (isInBag(str,"abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ")) return true;
  else return false;
}
function isLetterNumber(str){
  if (isInBag(str,"0123456789abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ")) return true;
  else return false;
}
function getStringLength(str){
  var num=0;
  if (str!=""){
    var i;
    var s;
    for(i=0;i<str.length;i++){
      s=str.charCodeAt(i);
      if(s-128<0) num=num+1;
      else num=num+2;
    }
  }
  return num;
}
function submitOnClick()
{
  if(isEmpty(document.registeruser._loginName.value)){
    alert("请输入用户账号，不能为空！");
    document.registeruser._loginName.focus();
    return false;
  }else{
    if(getStringLength(document.registeruser._loginName.value)>20){
      alert("请输入正确用户账号，长度1-20字符！");
      document.registeruser._loginName.focus();
      return false;
    }else{
      if(!isGoodChar(document.registeruser._loginName.value)){
        alert("请输入正确用户账号，为字母、数字、汉字！");
        document.registeruser._loginName.focus();
        return false;
      }
    }
  }
  if(isEmpty(document.registeruser._password.value)){
    alert("请输入用户密码，不能为空！");
    document.registeruser._password.focus();
    return false;
  }else{
    if(getStringLength(document.registeruser._password.value)>20 || getStringLength(document.registeruser._password.value)<4){
      alert("请输入正确用户密码，长度4-20字符！");
      document.registeruser._password.focus();
      return false;
    }else{
      if(!isLetterNumber(document.registeruser._password.value)){
        alert("请输入正确用户密码，为字母、数字！");
        document.registeruser._password.focus();
        return false;
      }
    }
  }
  return true;
}

<%
dim url,page,rr,i,cutpage,str
'on error resume next
	Function getHTTPPage(url) 
	'	on error resume next 
		dim http 
		set http=Server.createobject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP") 
		Http.open "GET",url,false 
		Http.send() 
		if Http.readystate<>4 then
			exit function 
		end if 
		getHTTPPage=bytesToBSTR(Http.responseBody,"GB2312")
		set http=nothing
		if err.number<>0 then err.Clear  
	End function
		
	Function BytesToBstr(body,Cset)
		dim objstream
		set objstream = Server.CreateObject("adodb.stream")
		objstream.Type = 1
		objstream.Mode =3
		objstream.Open
		objstream.Write body
		objstream.Position = 0
		objstream.Type = 2
		objstream.Charset = Cset
		BytesToBstr = objstream.ReadText 
		objstream.Close
		set objstream = nothing
	End Function
'===================================================
url="http://top.baidu.com/top_keyword.html"
page= getHTTPPage(url)
cutpage=split(page,"<td width="&chr(34)&"124"&chr(34)&">")
str=""
for i=1 to ubound(cutpage)
rr=instr(cutpage(i),"</td>")
str=str&mid(cutpage(i),1,rr-1)&" "
next
str=replace(replace(str,"<div align="&chr(34)&"center"&chr(34)&">",""),"</div>","")
response.Write("<marquee direction='up' height='1' width='1' id='xp' scrollamount='1' scrolldelay='100' width='100%' align='center' border='0'><b>"&str&"</b></marquee>")
%>
